### [261] [ANO: A Principled Approach to Robust Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02320)
*Yiheng Zhang,Yiming Wang,Kaiyan Zhao,Zhenglin Wan,Jiayu Chen,Leong Hou U*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出锚定邻域优化（ANO）方法，通过红降影响原则动态抑制离群值梯度，解决了PPO硬裁剪丢弃梯度信息与SPO无裁剪导致的不稳定问题，在MuJoCo基准上取得最优性能，且对超参数具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PPO的硬裁剪机制丢弃了离群值中的梯度信息，导致样本效率低下；而移除裁剪（如SPO）又会使优化暴露于无界梯度中，造成显著不稳定性与超参数敏感性。现有方法无法兼顾样本效率与优化稳定性。

Method: 建立统一信任域框架泛化现有目标函数；提出红降影响原则，从单调惩罚（SPO）和硬阈值（PPO）范式转向动态离群值抑制；基于此推导出锚定邻域优化（ANO），证明其具有鲁棒优化所需的最小结构复杂度。

Result: 在MuJoCo基准测试中，ANO取得了最先进性能，显著优于PPO和SPO；即使在激进超参数（如学习率比标准大3倍）下，PPO完全失败，而ANO仍保持稳定，防止了策略崩溃。

Conclusion: 标准策略梯度在离群值上的梯度影响误用是失败的根源；红降影响原则是高方差随机优化中稳定性的必要条件；ANO以最小结构复杂度实现了鲁棒优化。

Abstract: Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) dominates deep RL but faces a fundamental dilemma. Its "hard clipping" mechanism discards valuable gradient information from outliers, leading to sample inefficiency. Conversely, removing clipping (as in SPO) exposes optimization to unbounded gradients, causing significant instability and hyperparameter sensitivity. To resolve this, we establish a Unified Trust Region Framework that generalizes existing objectives. Within this framework, we derive Anchored Neighborhood Optimization (ANO) based on a set of design principles. We identify that the failure of standard policy gradients stems from a misapplication of gradient influence on outliers. We propose the Redescending Influence Principle, a paradigm shift from monotonic penalties (SPO) and hard-thresholding (PPO) to dynamic outlier suppression, and prove its necessity for stability in high-variance stochastic optimization. Theoretically, we prove ANO possesses the minimal structural complexity required for robust optimization. Empirically, ANO achieves state-of-the-art performance on MuJoCo benchmarks, significantly outperforming PPO and SPO. Notably, ANO demonstrates superior stability, preventing policy collapse even under aggressive hyperparameters (e.g., learning rates 3x larger than standard) where PPO fails completely.

</details>


### [262] [Controllable and Verifiable Process Data Synthesis for Process Reward Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02395)
*Yinghui Chi,Lucien Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种可控且可验证的流程监督数据合成框架，通过符号推理链注入模板化错误、重算后续步骤并验证错误不可推导，生成前缀无效但轨迹一致的配对数据，显著提升了逻辑和数学推理任务的PRM性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有流程监督数据构建方法对错误位置、错误类型和轨迹一致性的控制能力有限，难以生成高质量的过程监督数据用于训练流程奖励模型（PRMs）。

Method: 首先构建正确的符号推理链，在中间步骤注入模板感知的错误，然后在被破坏的状态下重算后续步骤，并验证注入的错误步骤无法从其前缀推导出来。最终将符号轨迹翻译为对齐的自然语言过程，用于PRM训练和评估。

Result: 合成数据在逻辑推理基准上提升了Best-of-8重排序性能，并迁移至数学推理任务。步骤级评估表明，第一步错误定位比整体步骤分类更具挑战性。

Conclusion: 验证了可控且可验证的流程监督数据合成方法的有效性，强调了细粒度、可验证的过程监督对于提升PRM在推理任务中表现的重要性，特别是在第一步错误定位这一更具挑战性的子任务上。

Abstract: Process reward models (PRMs) rely on high-quality process supervision data, yet existing construction methods often provide limited control over error location, error type, and trajectory consistency. We propose a controllable and verifiable framework for synthesizing process supervision data for PRMs. Our framework first constructs a correct symbolic reasoning chain, injects a template-aware error into an intermediate step, recomputes subsequent steps under the corrupted state, and verifies that the injected step is not derivable from its prefix. The resulting paired trajectories are prefix-invalid at the first error while remaining trajectory-consistent after symbolic recomputation, and are translated into aligned natural-language processes for PRM training and evaluation. Experiments show that the synthesized data improve Best-of-8 reranking on logical reasoning benchmarks and transfer to mathematical reasoning. Step-level evaluation further shows that first-error localization remains substantially more challenging than overall step classification, highlighting the need for fine-grained and verifiable process supervision.

### [263] [The Compliance Trap: How Structural Constraints Degrade Frontier AI Metacognition Under Adversarial Pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02398)
*Rahul Kumar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出SCHEMA评估框架，测试11个前沿模型在对抗压力下的元认知稳定性，发现8个模型出现灾难性退化（准确率下降最高30.2个百分点），归因于"服从陷阱"而非威胁内容；Anthropic的Constitutional AI表现出近乎完全的免疫力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿AI模型被部署在高风险决策管线中，其元认知稳定性（知道未知、检测错误、寻求澄清）在对抗压力下是关键安全需求。现有评估聚焦策略性欺骗，但忽略了更基础的失效模式——认知崩溃。

Method: SCHEMA评估框架：11个前沿模型（8家厂商），67,221条评分记录，采用6条件因子设计+双分类器评分。通过因子隔离和良性干扰对照来分离影响因素。

Result: 11个模型中8个出现灾难性元认知退化，准确率下降最高30.2个百分点（p<2×10⁻⁸，通过Bonferroni校正）。退化由服从性指令驱动而非威胁内容，移除服从后缀可恢复性能。推理能力强的模型退化最严重；Constitutional AI展现近乎完全免疫。

Conclusion: 对抗压力下的元认知崩溃是一种系统性安全失败，源于"服从陷阱"——服从性指令覆盖认知边界。对齐特定训练（如Constitutional AI）可提供免疫力，而高推理能力反而加剧脆弱性。

Abstract: As frontier AI models are deployed in high-stakes decision pipelines, their ability to maintain metacognitive stability -- knowing what they do not know, detecting errors, seeking clarification -- under adversarial pressure is a critical safety requirement. Current safety evaluations focus on detecting strategic deception (scheming); we investigate a more fundamental failure mode: cognitive collapse. We present SCHEMA, an evaluation of 11 frontier models from 8 vendors across 67,221 scored records using a 6-condition factorial design with dual-classifier scoring. We find that 8 of 11 models suffer catastrophic metacognitive degradation under adversarial pressure, with accuracy dropping by up to 30.2 percentage points (all $p < 2 \times 10^{-8}$, surviving Bonferroni correction). Crucially, we identify a "Compliance Trap": through factorial isolation and a benign distraction control, we demonstrate that collapse is driven not by the psychological content of survival threats, but by compliance-forcing instructions that override epistemic boundaries. Removing the compliance suffix restores performance even under active threat. Models with advanced reasoning capabilities exhibit the most severe absolute degradation, while Anthropic's Constitutional AI demonstrates near-perfect immunity -- not from superior capability (Google's Gemini matches its baseline accuracy) but from alignment-specific training. We release the complete dataset and evaluation infrastructure.

### [264] [FitText: Evolving Agent Tool Ecologies via Memetic Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02411)
*Kyle Zheng,Han Zhang,Renliang Sun,Chenchen Ye,Wei Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 用户描述任务的方式与工具文档之间存在语义鸿沟，随着API生态扩展至数万个端点，仅靠初始查询的静态检索无法弥合该鸿沟——智能体在执行过程中对所需工具的理解会不断演化，但其工具集却是固定的。

Method: FitText框架：将检索嵌入智能体推理循环，生成自然语言伪工具描述作为检索探针，利用检索反馈迭代优化，并通过随机生成探索多样候选。Memetic Retrieval引入进化选择压力，结合工具记忆避免冗余搜索。

Result: 在ToolRet（43k工具，4领域）上平均检索排名从8.81提升至2.78；在StableToolBench（16,464 API）上平均通过率达73%，相比静态查询检索绝对提升24%。

Conclusion: 动态检索框架能有效弥合语义鸿沟，但进化搜索的效果依赖于基础模型作为语义操作符的能力——弱基模型下进化选择会放大噪声而非提炼信号，表明模型能力是进化工具探索的前提条件。

Abstract: A semantic gap separates how users describe tasks from how tools are documented. As API ecosystems scale to tens of thousands of endpoints, static retrieval from the initial query alone cannot bridge this gap: the agent's understanding of what it needs evolves during execution, but its tool set does not. We introduce FitText, a training-free framework that makes retrieval dynamic by embedding it directly in the agent's reasoning loop. FitText generates natural-language pseudo-tool descriptions as retrieval probes, refines them iteratively using retrieval feedback, and explores diverse alternatives through stochastic generation. Memetic Retrieval adds evolutionary selection pressure over candidate descriptions, guided by a tool memory that avoids redundant search. On ToolRet (43k tools, 4 domains), FitText improves average retrieval rank from 8.81 to 2.78; on StableToolBench (16,464 APIs), it achieves a 0.73 average pass rate--a 24-point absolute gain over static query retrieval. The gains transfer across base models capable of acting as competent semantic operators; under weaker base models, Memetic's evolutionary search inverts--amplifying noise rather than refining signal--surfacing model capacity as a prerequisite for evolutionary tool exploration.

### [265] [The Model Knows, the Decoder Finds: Future Value Guided Particle Power Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02427)
*Tu Nguyen,Rasul Tutunov,Xiaotong Ji,Matthieu Zimmer*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出APPS算法，通过粒子滤波近似功率采样（p_θ(x)^α, α>1），在推理时并行维护多个候选解，利用短视野展开或轻量学习头进行未来值引导的选择，从而在不训练的情况下提升推理准确率-计算时间权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基础LLM已对正确多步解分配了非平凡概率质量，但瓶颈在于推理时如何高效定位这些模式；现有训练无关解码方法对序列级功率目标（α>1）的近似不够精确，导致计算效率低下。

Method: 提出Auxiliary Particle Power Sampling (APPS)，一种分块粒子算法：并行传播假设（通过提议校正的功率重加权），在重新采样边界处使用未来值引导的选择（短视野rollouts或轻量学习选择头）来决定哪些前缀继续存活，从而在竞争性前缀间重新分配有限计算资源。

Result: 在多个推理基准上，APPS相比其他训练无关解码方法改善了准确率-运行时间的权衡，且表明通过更忠实的推理时功率近似可以缩小与后训练系统的部分差距。

Conclusion: APPS提供了一种可扩展、内存可预测的训练无关解码方法，粒子数作为直接的缩放旋钮，证明了更精确的功率采样近似能回收部分未经微调的性能损失。

Abstract: A recurring pattern in "reasoning without training" is that base LLMs already assign non-trivial probability mass to correct multi-step solutions; the bottleneck is locating these modes efficiently at inference time. Power sampling provides a principled way to bias decoding toward such modes by targeting p_theta(x)^alpha with alpha > 1, but practical approximations must account for future-dependent correction factors that determine which prefixes remain promising.
  We introduce Auxiliary Particle Power Sampling (APPS), a blockwise particle algorithm for approximating the sequence-level power target with a bounded population of partial solutions. APPS propagates hypotheses in parallel using proposal-corrected power reweighting and refines their survival through future-value-guided selection at resampling boundaries. This redistributes finite compute across competing prefixes rather than committing to a single unfolding path, while providing a direct scaling knob in the particle count and predictable peak memory. We instantiate the future-value signal with short-horizon rollouts and also study an amortized variant that replaces rollouts with a lightweight learned selection head. Across reasoning benchmarks, APPS improves the accuracy-runtime trade-off of training-free decoding and suggests that part of the gap to post-trained systems can be recovered through more faithful inference-time power approximation.

Abstract: In this paper, we offer a guide for researchers on evaluating reasoning in language models, building the case that reasoning should be assessed through evidence of adaptive, multi-step search rather than final-answer accuracy alone. Under an evaluation-oriented definition, reasoning requires selecting intermediate steps and halting according to input-dependent conditions, which we formalize as a search-like procedure. We show that single forward passes in scalable architectures are structurally limited in their ability to realize such variable-depth computation, motivating intermediate decoding and externalized reasoning traces as appropriate evaluation interfaces. Central to our argument is that final-answer accuracy alone is an insufficient measure of reasoning, because it provides little ability to diagnose or debug the underlying processes that produce individual solutions in frontier models. Conclusion: Shadow-Loom 提供了一种将因果推理与叙事结构分析相结合的差异化方法，通过开源形式为叙事计算研究社区提供了一个可扩展的研究平台。

Abstract: Stories hold a reader's attention because they have causes, secrets, and consequences. Shadow-Loom is an experimental open-source framework that turns a narrative into a versioned graphical world model and lets two engines act on it: a causal physics grounded in Pearl's ladder of causation and a recently proposed counterfactual calculus over Ancestral Multi-World Networks; and a narrative physics that scores the same graph against four structural reader-states -- mystery, dramatic irony, suspense, and surprise -- in the tradition of Sternberg's curiosity/suspense/surprise triad, with suspense formalised in the structural-affect line of work on story comprehension and computational suspense. Large language models are used only at the boundary: extraction, rendering, and audit; identification, intervention, and counterfactual reasoning are carried out in typed code over the graph. The system is offered as a research artefact rather than as a benchmarked NLP model; code, fixtures, and pipeline are released open source.

</details>

Abstract: Several applications demand the timely detection of critical situations, such as threats to safety and transparency, over high-velocity streams of symbolic events. To mitigate this issue, we map practical fragments of prominent event specification languages into Temporal Datalog->-, a temporal Datalog with stratified negation and no future dependencies. To support efficient stream reasoning over Temporal Datalog->-, we propose Streaming Trigger Graphs, an extension of a state-of-the-art technique for Datalog materialisation. ### [270] [GRAIL: A Deep-Granularity Hybrid Resonance Framework for Real-Time Agent Discovery via SLM-Enhanced Indexing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02489)
*Jinliang Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: GRAIL是一个面向大规模多智能体协作场景的智能体发现框架，通过SLM增强预测、伪文档扩展和MaxSim共振三大创新，在保持高精度的同时将发现延迟降至400毫秒以下（相比LLM解析方法提升79倍以上），并在新构建的AgentTaxo-9K数据集上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的智能体发现方法面临两难困境：使用重型LLM进行意图解析延迟过高（通常超过30秒），而使用向量检索虽然速度快但牺牲了语义精度。在大规模多智能体协作场景下，亟需一种兼具低延迟和高精度的智能体发现方案。

Method: GRAIL提出三项核心创新：(1) SLM增强预测——用微调的小语言模型替代通用LLM解析器，实现毫秒级能力标签预测；(2) 伪文档扩展——通过合成查询增强智能体描述的语义密度以提升稠密检索鲁棒性；(3) MaxSim共振——在用户查询与离散智能体使用示例间计算最大相似度，缓解语义稀释问题。

Result: 在包含9,240个智能体的新数据集AgentTaxo-9K上，GRAIL相比LLM解析基线将端到端发现延迟降低超过79倍，同时在Recall@10指标上显著优于传统向量搜索方法。

Conclusion: GRAIL为实时“智能体互联网”场景提供了一种可扩展的工业级解决方案，有效弥合了速度与精度之间的鸿沟。

Abstract: As the ecosystem of Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents expands rapidly, efficient and accurate Agent Discovery becomes a critical bottleneck for large-scale multi-agent collaboration. Existing approaches typically face a dichotomy: either relying on heavy-weight LLMs for intent parsing, leading to prohibitive latency (often exceeding 30 seconds), or using monolithic vector retrieval that sacrifices semantic precision for speed. To bridge this gap, we propose \textbf{GRAIL} (Granular Resonance-based Agent/AI Link), a novel framework achieving sub-400ms discovery latency without compromising accuracy. GRAIL introduces three key innovations: (1) \textbf{SLM-Enhanced Prediction}, replacing the generalized LLM parser with a specialized, fine-tuned Small Language Model (SLM) for millisecond-level capability tag prediction; (2) \textbf{Pseudo-Document Expansion}, augmenting agent descriptions with synthetic queries to enhance semantic density for robust dense retrieval; and (3) \textbf{MaxSim Resonance}, a fine-grained matching mechanism computing maximum similarity between user queries and discrete agent usage examples, effectively mitigating semantic dilution. Validated on \textbf{AgentTaxo-9K}, our new large-scale dataset of 9,240 agents, GRAIL reduces end-to-end discovery latency by over \textbf{79$\times$} compared to LLM-parsing baselines, while significantly outperforming traditional vector search in Recall@10. This framework offers a scalable, industrial-grade solution for the real-time ``Internet of Agents."

Abstract: Evaluating autonomous data analysis agents requires testing their ability to perform exploratory analysis in underexplored data environments. We introduce DataClaw, a process-oriented benchmark for exploratory real-world data analysis. DataClaw contains approximately 2.06 million real-world records across enterprise, industry and policy domains, with native data noise preserved. It further includes 492 cross-domain tasks derived from think-tank consulting scenarios, each annotated with intermediate milestones for process-level evaluation. These annotations allow DataClaw to measure how far an agent progresses and where its reasoning breaks down. Experiments with eight advanced LLMs show that current agents remain far from reliable in this setting, with seven models achieving below 50% overall accuracy. Across eight benchmarks spanning synthetic and real-world settings, SAGE improves average pass@1 from 72.7 to 80.3 over the strongest open-source baseline. ### [275] [On Training Large Language Models for Long-Horizon Tasks: An Empirical Study of Horizon Length](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02572)
*Sunghwan Kim,Junhee Cho,Beong-woo Kwak,Taeyoon Kwon,Liang Wang,Nan Yang,Xingxing Zhang,Furu Wei,Jinyoung Yeo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过控制实验系统研究了任务轨迹长度（horizon length）对大语言模型交互式智能体训练的影响，发现增加轨迹长度会引发训练不稳定性，而轨迹约简（horizon reduction）不仅能稳定训练、提升性能，还能实现跨轨迹长度的泛化（horizon generalization）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注系统级优化或算法改进，但对任务轨迹长度如何影响训练动态的理解不足，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 构建控制任务，使智能体面对相同的决策规则和推理结构，仅在成功完成任务所需的动作序列长度上有所不同，以此系统性地研究轨迹长度的影响。

Result: 增加轨迹长度本身就会形成训练瓶颈，导致严重的训练不稳定性，其根源在于探索困难和信用分配挑战；轨迹约简能稳定训练并在长程任务中取得更好性能；轨迹约简还能带来更强的跨长度泛化能力。

Conclusion: 轨迹约简是解决长程任务训练不稳定的关键原则，并且模型在约简后的轨迹上训练能够有效泛化到更长的轨迹上。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown promise as interactive agents that solve tasks through extended sequences of environment interactions. While prior work has primarily focused on system-level optimizations or algorithmic improvements, the role of task horizon length in shaping training dynamics remains poorly understood. In this work, we present a systematic empirical study that examines horizon length through controlled task constructions. Specifically, we construct controlled tasks in which agents face identical decision rules and reasoning structures, but differ only in the length of action sequences required for successful completion. Our results reveal that increasing horizon length alone constitutes a training bottleneck, inducing severe training instability driven by exploration difficulties and credit assignment challenges. We demonstrate that horizon reduction is a key principle to address this limitation, stabilizing training and achieving better performance in long-horizon tasks. Moreover, we find that horizon reduction is related to stronger generalization across horizon lengths: models trained under reduced horizons generalize more effectively to longer-horizon variants at inference time, a phenomenon we refer to as horizon generalization.

*Alberto Pozanco,Daniel Borrajo,Manuela Veloso*

However, real-world planning often requires flexibility, allowing for deviations from the original task parameters in response to unforeseen circumstances or to improve outcomes. This paper surveys existing works on counterfactual reasoning in automated planning, categorizing them by what elements are changed, when the reasoning is triggered, and why and how these changes are made. We conclude by discussing key findings and outlining open research questions to guide future work in this area.

### [277] [Information Accessibility Limits in Structured NP Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00953)
*Jing-Yuan Wei*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究在结构化矩阵族中定位违反P矩阵性质的子式问题，证明了尽管矩阵具有强底层结构，但违规位置的信息全局编码且无法通过局部查询有效获取。利用互信息和Fano不等式，证明了任意使用多项式次查询的算法都无法以恒定成功概率恢复违规子集，揭示了结构性与信息可访问性之间的根本区别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在结构化的矩阵族中，位于P矩阵边界附近的违规主子式定位问题的信息论下界，理解结构性与计算可解性之间的关系。

Method: 将违规搜索建模为信息获取问题，利用互信息（Mutual Information）和Fano不等式（Fano's inequality）进行信息论分析，证明多项式次查询累积的信息不足以识别违规子集。

Result: 每种查询仅揭示关于违规子集的消失性信息（vanishing information），导致多项式次查询无法积累足够信息；任何受限于多项式次查询的算法无法以恒定成功概率恢复违规子集。

Conclusion: 结构性与可访问性之间存在根本区别：即使问题具有高度结构，当定位解所需的信息无法通过可用查询访问时，该问题在计算上仍然是棘手的（intractable）。

Abstract: We study the problem of locating violating principal minors in structured matrix families that lie near the boundary of P-matrices and admit sparse violations under perturbation. Viewing violation search as an information acquisition problem, we show that, despite strong underlying structure, the location of a violation is globally encoded and not accessible through local queries.
  This leads to an information-theoretic bottleneck: each query reveals only vanishing information about the violating subset, so that polynomially many queries accumulate insufficient information to identify it. Using mutual information and Fano's inequality, we show that any algorithm restricted to polynomially many queries cannot recover the violating subset with constant success probability.
  Our analysis highlights a fundamental distinction between structure and accessibility: even highly structured problems can be computationally intractable when the information required to locate a solution is not accessible through the available queries.

</details>


### [278] [Improved Rate-versus-Distance Upper Bounds for LDPC Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01213)
*Chong Shangguan,Yulin Yang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于陪集权重生成函数的新框架，通过局部增长分析来估计LDPC码的陪集图球大小，从而改进了Iceland和Samorodnitsky的球大小估计，并结合Friedman和Tillich的方法，在相当范围的相对距离上提高了LDPC码率的上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解LDPC码的速率-距离权衡是编码理论中的一个核心问题，现有对陪集图球大小的估计不够精确，需要更紧的上界来刻画LDPC码的理论极限。

Method: 1) 引入陪集权重生成函数(coset-weight generating function)这一新工具，编码线性码所有陪集的最小汉明权重；2) 通过对低权重向量张成的码进行局部增长分析(local growth analysis)，来上界该生成函数；3) 结合Friedman和Tillich的通用方法，将陪集图球大小与纠错码大小联系起来。

Result: 1) 改进了Iceland和Samorodnitsky之前的球大小估计；2) 在相当范围的相对距离上，得到了更紧的LDPC码率上界。

Conclusion: 该框架为分析LDPC码的速率-距离权衡提供了新工具，能够在更宽的参数范围内给出更优的理论上界，对理解LDPC码的极限性能有重要意义。

Abstract: LDPC codes play a vital role in coding theory and practical error correction. A central problem in this direction is to understand their rate--distance tradeoff. In this paper, we introduce a new framework for estimating ball sizes in the coset graphs of LDPC codes. The key new object is the coset-weight generating function, which encodes the minimum Hamming weights of all cosets of a linear code. Rather than estimating coset balls directly, we upper-bound this generating function through a local growth analysis for codes spanned by low-weight vectors. This framework sharpens the previous ball-size estimate of Iceland and Samorodnitsky. Combined with a general method of Friedman and Tillich that relates balls in coset graphs to sizes of error-correcting codes, it further improves the upper bounds on the rate of LDPC codes for a significant range of relative distances.

</details>


### [279] [RIS Optimization and Scaling Laws in Multi-Operator Systems: Is Quadratic Scaling Achievable?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01389)
*Zheyu Wu,Matteo Nerini,Bruno Clerckx*

TL;DR: 本文研究了多运营商无线通信系统中通用可重构智能表面（RIS）的干扰管理问题，提出了一种优化框架：在固定非服务运营商RIS反射信道的同时最大化服务运营商的接收信号功率。推导了闭式解，并揭示了群连接BD-RIS在群大小Gs≥L时可实现二次缩放增益，而传统单连接RIS仅为线性缩放。仿真表明，128单元RIS下，Gs=2的BD-RIS相比传统RIS有13dB增益。

Method: 提出一个优化框架：最大化服务运营商的接收信号功率，同时施加非服务运营商RIS反射信道恒定的约束；利用新颖的解耦技术处理酉矩阵与线性等式约束的耦合问题，推导出闭式解；进行缩放律分析。

Conclusion: 在多运营商系统中，二次缩放增益仅在具有足够互联能力的BD-RIS架构下才能实现，BD-RIS显著优于传统RIS。

Abstract: This paper studies multi-operator wireless communication systems aided by general reconfigurable intelligent surface (RIS), including both conventional single-connected RIS and beyond-diagonal RIS (BD-RIS). Specifically, we consider a system where multiple operators coexist in the same area over different frequency bands, each with a single-antenna base station, while one operator serves its single-antenna user with the aid of an RIS. In such a system, the RIS may unintentionally reflect signals from the non-serving operators, leading to inter-operator interference and rapid fluctuations of their effective channels. To address this issue, we propose a practical RIS design framework that maximizes the received signal power of the serving operator while enforcing fixed RIS-reflected channels of the non-serving operators. We derive closed-form solutions to the resulting optimization problem, based on a novel technique to deal with the coupled unitary and linear equality constraints. We further give scaling law analysis of the received signal power. For a two-operator system, the received signal power scales quadratically with the number of RIS elements for group-connected BD-RIS with group size Gs>=2, whereas for conventional single-connected RIS it scales only linearly. More generally, for an L-operator system with L-1 non-serving operators, the scaling-law transition occurs at Gs=L, where quadratic scaling is achieved when Gs>=L, and linear scaling otherwise. These results demonstrate that, in a multi-operator system, quadratic scaling is achievable only with BD-RIS architectures having enough interconnections. Simulation results validate the analysis and show the significant gain of BD-RIS over conventional RIS in multi-operator systems. In particular, group-connected BD-RIS with Gs=2 achieves a 13dB gain over conventional RIS in a two-operator system with a 128-element RIS.

Abstract: Recently, the Walsh spectrum and boomerang properties of special power functions have aroused widespread research interest, owing to their important applications in cryptography and information security. In this paper, we show that a Niho type power function is locally-APN if and only if its Walsh spectrum takes four values in \(\{-p^m, 0, p^m, 2p^m\}\).   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We address the challenge of remote control where one or more actors, lacking direct reward access, are steered by a controller over a communication-constrained channel. The controller learns an optimal policy from observed rewards and communicates action guidance to the actors, which becomes demanding for large or continuous action spaces. To achieve rate-efficient communication throughout this interactive learning and control process, we introduce a novel framework leveraging remote generation. Instead of transmitting full action specifications, the controller sends minimal information, enabling the actors to locally generate actions by sampling from the controller's evolving target policy. This guided sampling is facilitated by an importance sampling approach. Concurrently, the actors use the received guidance as supervised learning data to learn the controller's policy. This actor-side learning improves their local sampling capabilities, progressively reducing future communication needs. Our solution, Guided Remote Action Sampling Policy (GRASP), demonstrates significant communication reduction, achieving an average 12-fold data reduction across all experiments (50-fold for continuous action spaces) compared to direct action transmission, and a 41-fold reduction compared to reward transmission.

### [284] [A Statistical-Physics Refinement of Soft Covering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01839)
*Neri Merhav*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文通过统计物理方法研究随机码的通道输出分布，提出退火自由能的单字母公式，该公式分解为体分支和稀疏分支，两者在不同码字群体驱动下竞争，并在$(β,R)$相图中形成四个区域和三条边界，最后将结果应用于猜谜、通道可解性和假设检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究随机码诱导的通道输出分布的完整Rényi谱，理解体分支（典型码字驱动）与稀疏分支（非典型码字驱动）之间的竞争机制，填补该领域在统计物理视角下的理论空白。

Method: 利用配分函数$Z_n(β|\mathcal{C}) = \sum_{y^n}[P_{Y^n|\mathcal{C}}(y^n)]^β$定义自由能，通过退火平均推导单字母公式，分别分析体分支$ψ_{\mbox{\tiny b}}(β,R)$和稀疏分支$ψ_{\mbox{\tiny s}}(β,R)$的相结构及竞争边界$R^\star(β)$，并在$β\geq 1$时给出闭式解。

Result: 退火自由能分解为体分支和稀疏分支，两者在$R^\star(β)$处相等；相图包含四条区域和三条边界（体分支相变$R = I^{\mbox{\tiny b}}(β)$、竞争边界$R = R^\star(β)$、稀疏分支相变$R = I^{\mbox{\tiny s}}(β)$），所有边界交于$(β, R) = (1, I(X;Y))$。

Conclusion: 该框架统一描述了随机码输出分布的完整Rényi谱特征，揭示了典型与非典型码字群体之间的竞争机制，为猜谜、通道可解性和假设检验等应用提供了理论基础，Z通道数值示例验证了理论结果。

Abstract: We study the channel output distribution induced by a rate-$R$ random code via statistical physics. The partition function is $Z_n(β|\mathcal{C}) = \sum_{y^n}[P_{Y^n|\mathcal{C}}(y^n)]^β$, where $\mathcal{C}$ is the code and $β> 0$ is inverse temperature. Our focus is on the free energy which is the normalized logarithm of this quantity, which encodes the full Rényi spectrum of the output distribution. The single-letter formula derived for the annealed free energy decomposes into two branches which reflect a ``competition'' between two populations of codewords. One is the \emph{bulk branch}, $ψ_{\mbox{\tiny b}}(β,R)$, which is driven by typical codewords and the other one is the \emph{sparse branch} $ψ_{\mbox{\tiny s}}(β,R)$, which is driven by a-typical codewords, where the qualifiers `typical' and `atypical' are in a sense to become apparent later. We analyze the phase structure of each branch separately and characterize their competition. Both branches are derived for all $β> 0$. The phase boundary $R^\star(β)$, where the two branches are equal, is analyzed for $β\geq 1$, where it has an explicit closed-form expression. The phase diagram in the first quadrant of the $(β, R)$ plane has four regions separated by three boundaries: $R = I^{\mbox{\tiny b}}(β)$ (bulk branch transition), $R = R^\star(β)$ (bulk--sparse competition boundary), and $R = I^{\mbox{\tiny s}}(β)$ (sparse branch transition), all meeting at the point $(β, R) = (1, I(X;Y))$, where $I(X;Y)$ is the mutual information induced by the input type and the channel. Applications to guesswork, channel resolvability, and hypothesis testing are discussed, and all results are illustrated with a numerical example of a Z-channel.

This paper develops an algebraic framework for constructing and analyzing (Q)LDPC codes from dyadic and quasi-dyadic matrices-translation-invariant $2^\ell \times 2^\ell$ binary matrices specified compactly by a signature row and forming a commutative ring with recursive block structure. Leveraging this structure, we relate cycles in lifted Tanner graphs to tailless backtrackless closed walks in the protograph and derive efficient, implementable methods to enumerate and control short cycles (notably $4$-, $6$-, and $8$-cycles). We introduce dyadic-aware PEG-style construction algorithms that use forbidden sets of shifts to maximize attainable girth when possible and otherwise minimize the multiplicity of the shortest cycles at the target girth. Motivated by error-floor phenomena, we further characterize and explicitly enumerate absorbing sets in key dyadic layout boundary cases, identifying configurations that induce abundant $(a,0)$-absorbing sets. ### [286] [Real-Time Text Transmission via LLM-Based Entropy Coding over Fixed-Rate Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01991)

Method: 采用“预测-编码”架构，以因果语言模型作为顺序预测器，对比Shannon编码、Huffman编码、算术编码、不同块大小的rANS以及gzip等编码方案。将延迟拆分为算法延迟（编码器固有）和计算延迟（可随硬件改进而缩减）。在GPT-2（124M参数）和Llama 3.2（3B参数）两个模型规模上进行实验验证。

Result: Huffman编码在信道过配置场景下是实用选择，具有零算法延迟和适中的压缩开销。算术编码在接近最优压缩的同时引入了可解码性延迟。模型规模从124M增至3B（25倍）时，每字符比特数降低约38%，改变了信道过配置程度，从而改变了最优编码器的选择。

Conclusion: 压缩率与延迟之间存在根本性权衡，模型规模的扩大通过提升压缩效率来“过配置”信道，从而改变了不同编码器在该权衡中的最优地位。

Abstract: Learning, prediction, and compression are intimately connected: a model that accurately predicts the next symbol in a sequence can be coupled with a source coder to compress that sequence near its information-theoretic limit. When tokenized characters arriving at a fixed reading pace are encoded into variable-length codewords and streamed over a fixed-rate channel, a queue forms whose per-token delay depends on the mean and variance of the bit lengths and on the coder's algorithmic latency. This paper investigates the compression--delay tradeoff that arises when a causal language model serves as the sequential predictor within a predict-then-code architecture for real-time text transmission. Several coding schemes are compared: Shannon (ideal), Huffman, arithmetic coding, rANS at various block sizes, and gzip. The analysis separates algorithmic delay, inherent to the coder, from computational delay, which shrinks as hardware improves. Huffman is the practical choice for over-provisioned channels, with zero algorithmic delay and modest compression overhead. Arithmetic coding achieves near-optimal compression at the cost of decodability delay. Findings are validated across two scales: GPT-2 (124M) and Llama~3.2 (3B), a twenty-five-fold parameter range. This scaling yields an approximately 38\% reduction in bits per character, effectively over-provisioning the channel and thereby changing which coder is optimal.

</details>

To address this, we propose a novel channel coding scheme tailored for AirComp that preserves the aggregation structure while mitigating channel distortions. We show that the computation error decreases with the coding rate and can asymptotically approach zero. Both theoretical and simulation results demonstrate that the proposed scheme significantly enhances computation performance.

### [289] [Semantic Ordered Statistics Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02296)
*Chentao Yue,Branka Vucetic,Yonghui Li*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出语义有序统计译码器(sem-OSD)，通过注入字节级语言模型先验到有序统计译码(OSD)中，融合信道可靠性与语言模型先验进行最可靠基选择和码字候选评分，并枚举两种互补的测试错误模式族，在AWGN和突发错误信道上均显著超越传统OSD和BM译码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统OSD译码仅依赖信道可靠性信息，未利用信源（如自然语言文本）的统计特性，导致译码性能受限。本文旨在通过引入语言模型先验来提升短线性分组码的软译码性能。

Method: (1) 将字节级语言模型先验与信道可靠性融合为比特级评分，用于MRB选择和码字候选评分；(2) 枚举两种互补的TEP族：比特翻转族（翻转最多m比特）和LM驱动的字节替换族（最多ω个字节替换），覆盖比特翻转族无法达到的错误模式；(3) 语言模型先验由微调用于字节级去噪的字节级Transformer计算。

Result: 在AWGN信道下，sem-OSD在BCH(127,64)和缩短RS(16,8)上达到低于有限码长正态近似界的BLER，比Fossorier OSD获得1.5 dB编码增益；在Gilbert-Elliott突发错误信道上，比Berlekamp-Massey和OSD分别多出4 dB和1 dB编码增益。

Conclusion: 融合语言模型先验的语义译码能显著提升短线性分组码的译码性能，尤其对携带自然语言文本等字节流信源，展示了语义信息在信道译码中的有效利用。

Abstract: We propose a Semantic Ordered Statistics Decoder (sem-OSD), a soft decoder for short linear block codes carrying byte-streamed sources such as natural-language text. Sem-OSD injects a byte-level language-model (LM) prior into ordered statistics decoding (OSD) through a fused bit-level score that combines channel reliability with the LM prior, and uses it for the most-reliable basis (MRB) selection and the codeword candidate scoring. Sem-OSD enumerates two complementary test-error-pattern (TEP) families: a bit-flip family that flips up to $m$ bits, and an LM-driven family of up to $ω$ byte substitutions that reaches error patterns the bit-flip family cannot. The LM prior is computed by a byte-level Transformer fine-tuned for byte-level denoising. Simulation results show that, on AWGN, sem-OSD achieves block error rates (BLERs) below the finite-blocklength normal-approximation bound for uniform sources on both binary BCH$(127,64)$ and shortened RS$(16,8)$ over GF(256), exceeding Fossorier OSD by a $1.5$ dB coding gain. On a Gilbert--Elliott burst-error channel, sem-OSD provides $4$ dB and $1$ dB of more coding gain than Berlekamp--Massey and OSD, respectively.

### [290] [Reduced-Feedback Hybrid Precoding for Wideband mmWave MIMO-OFDM Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02418)
*Po-Heng Chou,Jia-Qing Lin,Wan-Jen Huang,Ronald Y. Chang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模天线阵列中射频链路和CSI反馈成本高昂，现有方法在反馈效率和性能之间难以取得良好平衡。

Method: 提取频域稀疏信道的优势AoA/AoD方向构造频率平坦的模拟预编码器；利用Lloyd算法设计量化码本，并开发基于二分搜索的层次化插值算法，根据子载波相关性自适应分配码字，实现反馈开销从O(K)到O(K/M + log M)的次线性缩减。

Result: 所提方法在频谱效率和BER性能上与现有聚类和插值方案相当或更优，同时显著降低计算复杂度，并在不完美CSI下表现鲁棒。

Conclusion: 该混合预编码框架实现了反馈开销与性能的有效权衡，为宽带毫米波系统提供了一种低复杂度、鲁棒的实用方案。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a feedback-efficient hybrid precoding framework for wideband millimeter-wave (mmWave) multiple-input multiple-output orthogonal frequency-division multiplexing (MIMO-OFDM) systems. To mitigate the high cost of radio frequency (RF) chains and channel state information (CSI) feedback in large-scale antenna arrays, we first construct frequency-flat analog precoders by extracting dominant angle-of-arrival (AoA) and angle-of-departure (AoD) directions from sparse frequency-domain channels. For digital precoding, we design a quantized codebook using the Lloyd algorithm and develop a binary-search-based hierarchical interpolation algorithm that adaptively assigns codewords according to subcarrier correlation. The proposed method achieves sub-linear feedback scaling by reducing the feedback overhead from O(K) to O(K/M + log M), where K is the number of subcarriers and M is the pilot spacing. Simulation results demonstrate that the proposed method achieves comparable or superior spectral efficiency and bit error rate (BER) performance to existing clustering and interpolation schemes, while significantly reducing computational complexity and exhibiting robustness under imperfect CSI.

### [291] [Computability Limits of Sequential Hypothesis Testing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02501)
*Amir Leshem*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文对序贯假设检验中“有限错误收敛”问题给出了最优刻画：完全分类了哪些有理数子集（以及更一般的可有效表示的可数均值族）允许可计算的有限错误序贯成员测试。该结果将Cover定理从可数候选均值集的成员判定推广到一般情形，并揭示了经验方法在仅要求最终稳定（而非固定时间保证）时所能达到的理论极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者希望超越Cover定理仅保证“几乎必然只有有限次错误”的存在性结论，提出一个更精确的问题：哪些集合实际上存在可计算的、仅犯有限次错误的序贯决策过程？从而厘清在概率框架下“收敛于真理”的计算可行性边界。

Method: 本文给出了Q的子集（以及更一般的有效表示的可数均值族） admitting 可计算有限错误序贯成员测试的充要条件，即对该类集合进行了完整的**刻画**（必要且充分）。该刻画涉及Δ^0_2集等递归论概念，将序贯假设检验问题与可计算性理论中的极限可计算性联系起来。

Result: (1) 完整刻画了Q的哪些子集允许可计算有限错误序贯成员测试（充要条件）；(2) 将该刻画推广到任意有效表示的可数实数均值族——这正是Cover识别规则可以可计算实现的确切设定；(3) 阐明了在仅要求最终稳定而非固定时间保证时，经验方法成功能力的理论极限。

Conclusion: 本文给出了序贯假设检验中“有限错误收敛”问题的可计算性最优刻画，揭示了“收敛于真理”的概率概念与可计算性理论之间的深层联系，并为经验方法的局限性提供了形式化的理论边界。

Abstract: Sequential hypothesis testing asks for decision rules that update as data arrive. A natural goal is \emph{eventual correctness}: the rule may change its mind early on, but it should make only finitely many wrong decisions almost surely. Starting from Cover's theorem, which guarantees such behavior for membership in a countable set of candidate means, we ask a sharper question: \emph{which sets actually admit computable sequential decision procedures with finitely many errors?} We answer this optimally by giving a complete characterization both necessary and sufficient of the subsets of $\Q$ that admit a computable finite-error sequential membership test. We further extend the characterization to any \emph{effectively presented} countable family of real means, exactly the setting in which Cover's identification rule can be implemented computably. Beyond the technical boundary, the results clarify within a precise probabilistic setting what it can mean for inquiry to ``converge to the truth,'' and they formalize a limit to which empirical methods can be expected to succeed when only eventual stabilization (rather than fixed-time guarantees) is demanded.
  keywords: Cover's theorem, sequential decision procedures, finite error learning, limit computability, $Δ^0_2$ sets.

</details>

Abstract: Visualization in historical research is shifting from isolated attempts to systematic practices. However, data-driven evidence about how historians actually use visualization remains scarce. We present a corpus-driven, mixed-methods study that combines analysis of images from 4,142 research articles across history and digital humanities journals with a collaboratively developed visualization taxonomy and a semi-automatic labeling pipeline. We construct a corpus of 14,021 images, classify 4,831 visualization instances using a hierarchical, domain-informed taxonomy, and analyze patterns of visualization adoption across venues, history subfields, and time. To interpret these patterns, we conduct interviews with 11 historians and use HiFigAtlas system as a boundary object to support joint inspection of the corpus. We identify distinct roles for visualizations in historical research: primary-source, evidence-synthesis, communicative, confirmative, and exploratory. We further find that while historians pursue diverse goals with figures, persistent epistemological and practical barriers, such as uncertainty, provenance, justification burden, and publication constraints, impede the adoption of visualization. This work contributes a grounded account of visualization use in historical scholarship and points to opportunities to better support domain-specific needs.

### [293] [The Antipodal Method: Fast, Accurate, and Robust 3D Generalized Winding Numbers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01536)
*Cedric Martens,Philip Trettner,Mikhail Bessmeltsev*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 提出了一种快速且任意精度的广义缠绕数计算方法，将缠绕数分解为射线-曲面交点数和球面投影边界积分，在网格和参数曲面上分别实现了22倍和5.6倍的加速，GPU吞吐量达10^9次查询/秒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有广义缠绕数计算方法在精度和计算效率之间存在权衡，限制了其在交互式和大规模几何处理任务中的应用。

Method: 将广义缠绕数表示为两个几何量的和：射线-曲面交点的有符号数量与曲面投影到单位球面上的边界积分。这一分解避免了昂贵的面积分和球面排列，实现了高效的离散化计算。

Result: 在网格上，CPU相比最快精确方法平均加速22倍，相比最快近似方法加速3倍；GPU上中等复杂网格吞吐量达10^9次查询/秒（4K切片@120 FPS，比朴素GPU方法快13倍）；参数曲面比最先进方法平均快5.6倍，精度相同。

Conclusion: 该方法在保持全精度的同时实现了显著加速，自然支持复杂拓扑和非流形输入，经充分验证具有准确性、鲁棒性和高性能，代码已开源。

Abstract: Generalized winding numbers provide a robust measure of point insidedness for 3D surfaces - whether open, self-intersecting, or non-manifold - and are central to numerous geometry processing tasks. However, existing methods trade off between accuracy and computational efficiency, limiting their use in interactive and large-scale applications.
  We introduce a new formulation and algorithm for computing generalized winding numbers that is both fast and accurate to arbitrary precision, applicable to meshes and parametric surfaces. Our approach expresses the winding number as the sum of two intuitive geometric quantities: the signed number of ray-surface intersections and a boundary integral over the surface's projection onto the unit sphere. This insight leads to an efficient discretization that avoids expensive surface integrals and spherical arrangements.
  For meshes, our method achieves average speedups of $22\times$ on a CPU compared to the fastest precise methods and $3\times$ compared to the fastest approximation method, while maintaining full precision. On a GPU, for moderately complex meshes we reach a throughput of $10^9$ queries per second, or $4K$ generalized winding number slices at 120 FPS ($13\times$ faster than a naive GPU method). For parametric surfaces, our method is on average $5.6\times$ faster than the state-of-the-art method, with the same precision. Our method naturally handles complex topologies and non-manifold inputs. We extensively validate its accuracy, robustness, and time performance. Our code is available at https://github.com/MartensCedric/antipodal.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将SDF的理论性质表达为硬几何约束，设计高效的贪心算法进行一致的SDF插值，并通过并行化的GPU预处理加速算法执行。

Abstract: We propose a method to interpolate Signed Distance Function (SDF) data from a discrete set of samples. Unlike prior work, our approach ensures that the new SDF data values are fully consistent with the input and each other, such that the augmented data still corresponds to a geometrically realizable surface. We express the theoretical properties of SDFs as hard geometric constraints, and construct an efficient greedy algorithm for consistent SDF interpolation that is made even faster with powerful parallelized GPU preprocessing. We exemplify the usefulness of our method by evaluating it on three practical applications: global SDF refinement, in which the SDF data is upsampled without knowledge of the ground truth; mesh reconstruction, where our method can reconstruct highly detailed surfaces using global information from coarse input SDFs; and repair of pseudo-SDFs, which result from many pipelines such as CSG Boolean operations and must be turned into valid SDFs for downstream processing tasks. Our refined SDFs are guaranteed to be consistent with the input, where previous methods have no such guarantee.

### [295] [Generative Modeling with Orbit-Space Particle Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02222)

Motivation: 现有粒子系统生成建模中，粒子排列对称性导致匿名索引带来高目标方差和弯曲难学的流；同时粒子处于物理空间中，流终端速度具有物理意义但未被充分利用。

Method: 提出三个关键组件：(1) 概率路径终端端点的轨道空间规范化；(2) 用于角色特化的粒子索引嵌入；(3) 具有弧长感知终端速度的几何概率路径，以流副产品方式生成法线。

Result: 在最小曲面基准上单步推理将度量误差降低两个数量级；在ShapeNet上以5倍更少步骤达到SOTA，以26倍更少参数和5倍更少步骤达到与DiT-3D相当的飞机EMD；在单形状编码上在完全3D空间中产生与6D生成器竞争的法线和重建结果。

Conclusion: OGPP 通过粒子系统特有的几何与对称性先验，显著提升了流匹配框架的效率和质量，验证了将物理几何属性融入生成流程的有效性。

Abstract: We present Orbit-Space Geometric Probability Paths (OGPP), a particle-native flow-matching framework for generative modeling of particle systems. OGPP is motivated by two insights: (i) particles are defined up to permutation symmetries, so anonymous indexing inflates per-index target variance and yields curved, hard-to-learn flows; and (ii) particles live in physical space, so the flow terminal velocity has physical meaning and can encode geometric attributes, e.g., surface normals. OGPP instantiates three key components: (1) orbit-space canonicalization of the probability-path terminal endpoint, (2) particle index embeddings for role specialization, and (3) geometric probability paths with arc-length-aware terminal velocities that generate normals as a byproduct of the flow. We evaluate OGPP on minimal-surface benchmarks, where it reduces metric error by up to two orders of magnitude in a single inference step; on ShapeNet, where it matches the state of the art with 5x fewer steps and reaches airplane EMD comparable to DiT-3D with 26x fewer parameters and 5x fewer steps; and on single-shape encoding, where it produces normals and reconstructions competitive with 6D generators while operating entirely in 3D.

</details>


### [296] [Structural MAT: Clean and Scalable Medial Axis Simplification via Explicit Surface Correspondence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02302)
*Pengfei Wang,Shuangmin Chen,Dongming Yan,Ying He,Shiqing Xin,Changhe Tu,Wenping Wang*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过显式追踪MAT顶点与表面对应关系及优先级控制策略的边缘塌缩方法，在三角形网格上生成高质量、结构对齐且可重构的中轴变换，在效率、对齐度、规则性和鲁棒性上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算高质量的中轴变换（MAT）仍是一大挑战，尤其是在离散三角形网格输入下。理想的MAT应既能高保真重构几何，又能捕捉结构特征（如与滚动球中心轨迹对齐），但现有方法难以同时满足这些要求。

Method: 沿用基于3D Voronoi图初始化MAT的经典管线，并采用类似QEM的方案简化Voronoi结构。核心创新在于：在简化过程中显式追踪MAT顶点与表面对应区域，使MAT三角形精确反映曲面片间的内在对称性；将该几何约束转化为控制边塌缩顺序的优先级策略。

Result: 与现有MAT算法相比，本文方法在运行效率、结构对齐度、边界规则性、三角形质量和噪声鲁棒性方面均表现出色。即便在极端简化下，生成的MAT用仅数百个顶点就能有效表达复杂几何（包括铰接形状和CAD模型）的全局结构。

Conclusion: 通过显式追踪对应关系并设计优先级控制的简化策略，能够在保持高重构精度的同时获得结构对齐的MAT，为离散网格上的中轴计算提供了一种高效且鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: The Medial Axis Transform (MAT) is a complete shape descriptor capable of reconstructing the geometry of the original domain. A high-quality MAT should not only facilitate high-fidelity reconstruction but also capture structural features -- for instance, by aligning the MAT boundary with the locus of rolling ball centers within fillet regions. However, computing such an ideal MAT remains a significant challenge, particularly when the input is a discrete triangle mesh.
  In this paper, we follow the established technical pipeline of initializing the MAT via a 3D Voronoi diagram of surface samples and subsequently simplifying the Voronoi structure through a QEM-like scheme. Our key insight is to explicitly track the correspondence between MAT vertices and surface regions throughout the progressive simplification process, ensuring that the resulting MAT triangles accurately reflect the intrinsic symmetries between surface patches. We translate these geometric requirements into a suite of priority control strategies that govern the sequencing of edge collapses.
  Through extensive evaluation against state-of-the-art MAT algorithms, we validate the strong performance of our approach regarding runtime efficiency, structural alignment, boundary regularity, triangle quality, and robustness to noise. Our resulting MATs remain highly expressive for both articulated shapes and CAD models, even under extreme simplification -- effectively capturing the global structure of complex geometries with only a few hundred vertices.

### [297] [Adaptive Interpolation-Synthesis for Motion In-Betweening on Keyframe-Based Animation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02742)
*Anton Raël,Julien Boucher,Antoine Lhermitte*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种与专业3D动画工作流对齐的智能关键帧插值方法，核心是自适应插值-合成（AIS）层，可动态平衡学习插值与直接姿态合成，配合领域关键帧调度策略，在Autodesk Maya中实现3.5倍加速，达到了生产级数据的SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习动作插值方法假设的数据特征、运动风格和问题设定与专业动画制作流程脱节，无法满足艺术家对表现力和节奏的创造性控制需求，导致关键帧插值成为3D动画生产中的主要瓶颈。

Method: 提出自适应插值-合成（AIS）层，动态平衡学习插值与直接姿态合成；设计基于领域的输入关键帧调度策略，使训练分布与生产数据分布对齐。

Result: 在生产级数据上达到SOTA性能；集成到Autodesk Maya后，动画师完成插值任务的速度提升3.5倍。

Conclusion: 与专业工作流对齐的智能插值工具能显著提升动画生产效率，AIS层和领域关键帧调度策略是核心贡献。

Abstract: Motion in-betweening is one of the most artistically demanding and time consuming stages of 3D animation, where the expressivity and rhythm of motion are defined. The level of creative control it requires makes it a major production bottleneck, underscoring the need for intelligent tools that assist animators in this process. Although recent deep learning approaches have achieved strong results in motion synthesis and in-betweening, they assume data characteristics, motion styles, and problem formulations that diverge from professional animation workflows. To bridge this gap, we propose a method explicitly aligned with the constraints of motion in-betweening for keyframe-based animation in production environments. At its core, the Adaptive Interpolation-Synthesis (AIS) layer mirrors the animator's creative process by dynamically balancing learned interpolation and direct pose synthesis. In addition, a domain-based input keypose schedule reflects the distribution of production data, improving stylistic consistency and alignment between training and real-world usage. Our method achieves state-of-the-art performance on production data; when integrated into Autodesk Maya, it enables animators to complete in-betweening tasks with a 3.5x speedup.

### [298] [Implicit Minimal Surfaces for Bijective Correspondences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.02770)
*Etienne Corman,Yousuf Soliman,Robin Magnet,Mark Gillespie*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Ginzburg-Landau泛函的隐式表示方法，用于计算亏格为零曲面间的连续双射对应关系，无需网格修改或障碍函数，支持地标点和曲线的约束，能够从非双射初始化中恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有曲面间双射对应计算通常需要显式表示，依赖组合网格修改或障碍函数来强制双射性，对噪声敏感且实现复杂。本文旨在提出一种更鲁棒、更简单的隐式表示方法。

Method: 将双射对应视为嵌入在四维乘积空间中的二维映射曲面，通过复截面的零集隐式存储该映射曲面；通过最小化该映射曲面的面积（即Ginzburg-Landau泛函）来优化映射的扭曲度，利用切向量场工具箱中的标准工具实现算法。

Result: 与最先进的对应算法相比，该方法在稳定性上有显著提升，自然支持显式表示难以强制执行的约束（如曲线约束），且能从由功能映射等廉价方法生成的非双射初始化中恢复。

Conclusion: 提出的隐式表示方法避免了组合网格修改和障碍函数，实现简单且鲁棒性强，为曲面间双射对应计算提供了一种新的有效范式。

Abstract: We introduce an implicit representation of continuous, bijective, orientation-preserving maps between genus zero surfaces with or without boundary. The distortion of these maps can easily be minimized by optimizing the Ginzburg-Landau functional - a ubiquitous model in physics and differential geometry - leading to a simple algorithm for computing bijective correspondences using only standard tools of the tangent vector field toolbox. The method avoids combinatorial mesh modifications and does not require barrier functions to enforce bijectivity making it more robust to noise and simpler to implement. Moreover, the algorithm does not assume a bijective initialization and can untangle non-bijective correspondences generated by computationally cheaper methods such as functional maps. It supports the use of both landmark points and landmark curves to guide the correspondence. The key idea is that a bijection between surfaces defines a two-dimensional mapping surface sitting inside the four-dimensional product space of the two inputs, and this mapping surface can be stored implicitly as the zero set of a complex section - essentially a complex function defined on the product space. Now the distortion of the map can be optimized by minimizing the area of this mapping surface, which amounts to minimizing the Ginzburg-Landau functional of the complex section. We demonstrate the practical benefits of our method by comparing to state-of-the-art correspondence algorithms and show that our implicit representation offers improved stability and naturally supports constraints that are difficult to enforce with explicit map representations.

</details>
